## USER (2026-07-22 04:55:51)

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   - User wants to completely overhaul bash/neuron/ scripts using Docker environment (browsecomp-neuron:0.21.0) and vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0
   - Three models: Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B (planning, MoE), Qwen3-32B (judge, dense), Qwen3-Embedding-8B (embedding)
   - Hardware: trn2.3xlarge — 1 Neuron device × 4 cores, TP_SIZE=4
   - Models run sequentially (only one at a time)
   - User asked to automatically iterate on compile errors until it runs >5 minutes
   - Most recently: "又出问题了，你来解决一下" — fix the latest compilation error

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 breaking changes from NxDI/0.16.0 (config format, env vars, scheduler)
   - `NEURON_RT_VISIBLE_CORES` is deprecated; replaced by `NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES` (device-level, not core-level)
   - On trn2.3xlarge (1 device, 4 cores), don't set `NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES` at all — let vLLM auto-detect
   - TP_SIZE=4 counts NeuronCores, not devices
   - `NEURON_SKIP_EFA_AFFINITY=1` required on instances without EFA (trn2.3xlarge)
   - `num_batched_tokens_buckets` last value must equal `max_num_batched_tokens` (2048 when MAX_NUM_SEQS=1)
   - vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 model registry only has: LlamaForCausalLM, GptOssForCausalLM, Eagle3LlamaForCausalLM, Qwen3VLForConditionalGeneration
   - `--hf-overrides '{"architectures": ["GptOssForCausalLM"]}'` forces unsupported archs through the generic GptOss path
   - GptOssForCausalLM uses fused qkv_proj with weight mapping from HF's separate q/k/v keys
   - Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B (Qwen3MoeForCausalLM) has `attention_bias: False` — no bias tensors in checkpoint

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **bash/neuron/config/tongyi.env** — Tongyi model configuration (current state):
     ```bash
     # Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B Configuration
     # vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 | trn2.3xlarge (4 cores)
     MODEL="Alibaba-NLP/Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B"
     TP_SIZE=4
     MAX_MODEL_LEN=32768
     MAX_NUM_SEQS=1
     # Compilation
     VLLM_NEURON_PARALLEL_COMPILE_WORKERS=4
     NEURON_SKIP_EFA_AFFINITY=1
     # Runtime
     BLOCK_SIZE=32
     NUM_GPU_BLOCKS_OVERRIDE=4000
     # Paths
     NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS="local-models/neuron-compiled-artifacts/tongyi-32k-tp4-v0.21.0"
     VLLM_CACHE_ROOT="local-models/vllm-cache"
     VLLM_NEURON_LOG_LEVEL=INFO
     ```

   - **bash/neuron/config/judge.env** — Judge model configuration (same pattern, MODEL="Qwen/Qwen3-32B", MAX_MODEL_LEN=8192, BLOCK_SIZE=128, NUM_GPU_BLOCKS_OVERRIDE=2048)

   - **bash/neuron/config/tongyi_neuron_config.json** — Current state:
     ```json
     {
       "neuron_config": {
         "num_batched_tokens_buckets": [2048],
         "num_seqs_buckets": [1],
         "kv_segment_size_buckets": [2048]
       }
     }
     ```

   - **bash/neuron/compile_tongyi.bash** — Current state includes:
     - Sources config/tongyi.env
     - Docker detection
     - Reads tongyi_neuron_config.json as ADDITIONAL_CONFIG
     - Exports: VLLM_NEURON_PARALLEL_COMPILE_WORKERS, NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS, VLLM_CACHE_ROOT, VLLM_NEURON_LOG_LEVEL, NEURON_SKIP_EFA_AFFINITY
     - Conditionally exports NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES
     - Calls vllm with `--hf-overrides '{"architectures": ["GptOssForCausalLM"]}'`
     - Port 9999

   - **bash/neuron/serve_tongyi.bash** — Same pattern but with `exec`, PORT env var (default 6008), `--host 0.0.0.0`

   - **bash/neuron/compile_judge.bash** and **serve_judge.bash** — Same pattern as tongyi variants

   - **bash/neuron/serve_tongyi_cluster.bash** and **serve_judge_cluster.bash** — Multi-replica with DEVICES_PER_REPLICA and NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES per replica

   - **vllm_neuron model registry** (read-only, at `/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/registry.py`):
     ```python
     models = [
         ("LlamaForCausalLM", LlamaForCausalLM),
         ("GptOssForCausalLM", GptOssForCausalLM),
         ("Eagle3LlamaForCausalLM", Eagle3LlamaForCausalLM),
         ("Qwen3VLForConditionalGeneration", Qwen3VLForConditionalGeneration),
     ]
     ```

   - **GptOss weight mapping** (line ~2261 in model_bf16.py) — Always maps `qkv_proj_bias` to `[q_proj.bias, k_proj.bias, v_proj.bias]` — fails when model has no attention bias

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **Error 1: NEURON_RT_VISIBLE_CORES not supported**
     - Fix: Replaced with NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES in configs and scripts; then removed entirely from .env (only set conditionally by cluster scripts)
   - **Error 2: assert len(neuron_visible_devices) == num_local_ranks**
     - Fix: Don't set NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES at all for single-model runs; only export conditionally
   - **Error 3: No EFA device found**
     - Fix: Added `NEURON_SKIP_EFA_AFFINITY=1` to both .env files and export in all scripts
   - **Error 4: Last bucket must equal max_num_batched_tokens (2048), got 4096**
     - Fix: Changed tongyi_neuron_config.json: `num_batched_tokens_buckets: [2048]`, `kv_segment_size_buckets: [2048]`
   - **Error 5: 'Qwen3MoeForCausalLM' has no attribute 'from_configs'**
     - Fix: Added `--hf-overrides '{"architectures": ["GptOssForCausalLM"]}'` to all compile and serve scripts
   - **Error 6 (CURRENT/UNRESOLVED): Checkpoint key(s) not found for 'model.layers.0.self_attn.qkv_proj_bias'**
     - Root cause: GptOssForCausalLM unconditionally maps qkv_proj_bias → [q_proj.bias, k_proj.bias, v_proj.bias], but Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B has `attention_bias: False` (no bias tensors in checkpoint)
     - This is a fundamental incompatibility between GptOss weight loader and Qwen3Moe architecture
     - NOT YET FIXED

5. Problem Solving:
   - Solved errors 1-5 through iterative debugging via tmux pane inspection
   - Error 6 is the current blocker: vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0's GptOssForCausalLM always expects attention bias in the checkpoint. Qwen3Moe doesn't have it (`attention_bias: False`).
   - Possible solutions to explore:
     - Check if GptOss model_bf16.py has a `strict=False` option or bias-optional path
     - Check if there's a config option to disable bias in GptOss model
     - The GptOss model might work for Qwen3-32B (dense) since Qwen3ForCausalLM might have attention_bias=True
     - May need to fall back to an older vLLM version or use a different approach for the MoE model

[{'tool_use_id': 'toolu_bdrk_01QnvgxBhdeYUZevLAULVGgA', 'type': 'tool_result', 'content': '# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\nimport torch\n\nfrom vllm_neuron.utils.weight_loader import SafetensorsWeightLoader\n\n\ndef fused_qkv_weight_loader(\n    q_size: int,\n    kv_size: int,  # This should be kv_size PER RANK (num_kv_heads_per_rank * head_dim)\n    shard_dim: int,\n    num_shards: int,\n    num_kv_heads: int,\n    head_dim: int,\n    hidden_size: int,\n    num_kv_replicas: int = 1,\n    kv_num_shards: int | None = None,\n) -> SafetensorsWeightLoader:\n    """\n    Create a SafetensorsWeightLoader that fuses Q, K, V weights with per-tensor sharding.\n\n    Args:\n        kv_num_shards: Number of shards for KV (defaults to num_shards).\n            When attention DP is enabled and kv_needs_a2a is False, KV is sharded\n            across TP only (kv_num_shards=tp_size) while Q is sharded across\n            TP*attention_dp (num_shards=tp_size*attention_dp_size).\n    """\n    kv_shards = kv_num_shards if kv_num_shards is not None else num_shards\n\n    # Calculate KV heads per rank based on KV-specific shard count\n    if kv_shards >= num_kv_heads:\n        num_kv_heads_per_rank = 1\n    else:\n        num_kv_heads_per_rank = num_kv_heads // kv_shards\n\n    kv_size_per_rank = num_kv_heads_per_rank * head_dim\n\n    def _pad_hidden(tensor: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:\n        """Pad dim 1 (in_features/hidden) to expecthidden_sizeed_hidden_size."""\n        pad_amount = hidden_size - tensor.shape[1]\n        if pad_amount <= 0:\n            return tensor\n        return torch.nn.functional.pad(tensor, (0, pad_amount))\n\n    def transform(slices: list, rank: int) -> torch.Tensor:\n        assert len(slices) == 3, (\n            "fused_qkv_weight_loader expects [Q, K, V] slices in order"\n        )\n\n        q_slice, k_slice, v_slice = slices\n\n        # Q is always sharded normally across all ranks\n        q_start = rank * q_size\n        q_end = q_start + q_size\n\n        # Determine KV head range for this rank.\n        # When kv_num_shards differs from num_shards (attention DP with kv_needs_a2a=False),\n        # derive the KV-specific rank from the Q rank.\n        if kv_shards != num_shards:\n            # rank is effective_q_rank (interleaved). KV rank is TP-based.\n            tp_rank_for_kv = rank // (num_shards // kv_shards)\n            kv_replicas_for_kv = max(kv_shards // num_kv_heads, 1)\n            kv_rank = tp_rank_for_kv // kv_replicas_for_kv\n        else:\n            kv_rank = rank // num_kv_replicas\n\n        # Checkpoint stores [out_features, in_features]\n        q_tensor = _pad_hidden(q_slice[q_start:q_end, :])\n\n        if kv_shards >= num_kv_heads:\n            # Each rank gets 1 KV head (possibly padded for extra ranks)\n            if kv_rank < num_kv_heads:\n                kv_start = kv_rank * head_dim\n                kv_end = kv_start + head_dim\n                k_tensor = _pad_hidden(k_slice[kv_start:kv_end, :])\n                v_tensor = _pad_hidden(v_slice[kv_start:kv_end, :])\n            else:\n                # Padded KV\n                k_tensor = torch.zeros(head_dim, hidden_size, dtype=q_tensor.dtype)\n                v_tensor = torch.zeros(head_dim, hidden_size, dtype=q_tensor.dtype)\n        else:\n            # Each rank gets MULTIPLE KV heads\n            kv_start = kv_rank * kv_size_per_rank\n            kv_end = kv_start + kv_size_per_rank\n            k_tensor = _pad_hidden(k_slice[kv_start:kv_end, :])\n            v_tensor = _pad_hidden(v_slice[kv_start:kv_end, :])\n\n        result = torch.cat([q_tensor, k_tensor, v_tensor], dim=0)\n\n        # We transpose since the QKV weight in the model is transposed from the original [out_features, in_features]\n        return result.T.contiguous()\n\n    return SafetensorsWeightLoader(transform=transform)\n\n\ndef fused_qkv_bias_loader(\n    q_size: int,\n    kv_size: int,\n    num_shards: int,\n    num_kv_heads: int,\n    head_dim: int,', 'is_error': False}]

Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B (Qwen3MoeForCausalLM) — TP=4, 32K context\n2. Qwen3-32B (Judge, Qwen3ForCausalLM) — TP=4, 8K context\n3. Qwen3-Embedding-8B — Optimum Neuron（不走vLLM）\n\n### **关键阻塞问题：attention_bias 不兼容**\n\n**现状：**\n- vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 的模型注册表只有 4 个架构：`LlamaForCausalLM`, `GptOssForCausalLM`, `Eagle3LlamaForCausalLM`, `Qwen3VLForConditionalGeneration`\n- **不支持** `Qwen3MoeForCausalLM` (Tongyi) 和 `Qwen3ForCausalLM` (Judge)\n- 通过 `--hf-overrides \'{"architectures": ["GptOssForCausalLM"]}\'` 可以强制使用 GptOss 通用路径\n- **但是**：GptOss 的 Attention 层**无条件初始化** `qkv_proj_bias` 和 `o_proj_bias` 参数，并在权重加载时**硬编码映射**到 HF checkpoint 的 `q_proj.bias`, `k_proj.bias`, `v_proj.bias`, `o_proj.bias` 键\n- Qwen3 系列所有模型的 config 中 `attention_bias: False` — checkpoint 中**不存在这些 bias 张量**\n- 加载时报错：`RuntimeError: Checkpoint key(s) not found for parameter \'model.layers.0.self_attn.qkv_proj_bias\': [\'model.layers.0.self_attn.q_proj.bias\', ...]`\n\n**根本原因：**\n- `/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/model_bf16.py` line ~398: `self.qkv_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(qkv_size, dtype=self.dtype))` — 无条件创建\n- line ~2267: `mappings[f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.qkv_proj_bias"] = [q_proj.bias, k_proj.bias, v_proj.bias]` — 无条件映射\n- GptOss config (`/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/config.py`) **没有 `attention_bias` 字段**\n- **GptOss 模型设计时假设所有模型都有 attention bias**，不支持 bias-free 架构'}}]

```python\n     if config.attention_bias:\n         self.qkv_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(qkv_size, dtype=self.dtype))\n         self.o_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(self.hidden_size, ```python\n     if config.attention_bias:\n         mappings[f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.qkv_proj_bias"] = [...]\n         mappings[f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.o_proj_bias"] = (...)\n     ```\n\n3. **`/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/weight_loaders_bf16.py`**\n   - `fused_qkv_bias_loader` 和权重加载器注册逻辑保持不变（当 bias=None 时不会调用）\n\n**实施方式：**\n\na. **Docker 镜像外部挂载 patch**（推荐，非侵入式）\n   - 在宿主机创建 `docker/patches/vllm_neuron/` 目录\n   - 复制原始文件并修改\n   - Docker compose 挂载：`-v ./docker/patches/vllm_neuron:/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron:ro`\n   - **优点**：不修改镜像，可版本控制，易于迭代\n   - **缺点**：每次拉新镜像需要重新验证 patch 兼容性\n\nb. **构建自定义 Docker 镜像**（生产级）\n   - `FROM public.ecr.aws/neuron/vllm-neuron:0.21.0`\n   - Dockerfile 中 `COPY patches/` + `RUN sed -i` 或直接 `COPY` 完整修改后的文件\n   - **优点**：自包含，可分发\n   - **缺点**：需要维护 Dockerfile，镜像体积增大\n\nc. **容器内运行时 patch**（调试用）\n   - `docker exec` 进容器，直接 `vim` 或 `sed -i` 修改文件\n   - **优点**：快速验证\n   - **缺点**：容器重启丢失，不可复现\n\n**风险评估：**\n\n- **低风险区域**：\n  - Config 增加字段（向后兼容，默认值 `True` 保持现有行为）\n  - Weight mapping 条件化（只影响 bias=False 的模型）\n  - Bias 初始化条件化（nn.Parameter 为 None 是合法的）\n\n- **中等风险**：\n  - Forward 中 XLA 算子调用改动 — 需要验证 `bias=None` 是否被 XLA kernel 支持\n  - 如果 `xla_attn` 不支持 `bias=None`，可能需要传 `torch.zeros_like(...)` 而非 None\n\n- **需要验证**：\n  - XLA attention kernel (`xla_attn`, `xla_attn_v3`) 是否支持 `bias=None` 或需要显式零张量\n  - Neuron 编译器是否会因 bias=None 优化掉相关计算\n  - TP 分片逻辑在 bias=None 时是否正常工作\n\n### 方案 B：实现独立 Qwen3Moe 模型类（完整支持）\n\n**目标：** 注册新的 `Qwen3MoeForCausalLM` 架构到 vLLM-Neuron\n\n**需要新增的文件：**\n\n1. **`/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/qwen3_moe/`**\n   - `config.py` — Qwen3Moe 配置（基于 GptOss 修改，增加 MoE 参数）\n   - `model_bf16.py` — Qwen3Moe 模型实现\n     - Attention 层：从 GptOss 复制并移除 bias\n     - **MoE 层**：需要实现 expert routing + top-k gating + load balancing\n   - `weight_loaders_bf16.py` — 权重加载器（复制 GptOss，移除 bias 映射）\n   - `factory.py` — 模型工厂\n   - `__init__.py` — 导出 `Qwen3MoeForCausalLM`\n\n2. **修改 `/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/registry.py`**\n   ```python\n   from .qwen3_moe import Qwen3MoeForCausalLM\n   models.append(("Qwen3MoeForCausalLM", Qwen3MoeForCausalLM))\n   ```\n\n**工作量：**\n\n- **Attention 层**：100 行（复制 GptOss，删 bias 逻辑）\n- **MoE 层**：300-500 行（expert routing, gating, load balancing, TP sharding）\n- **Config + 权重映射**：100 行\n- **XLA/Neuron kernel 适配**：未知（如果 MoE 需要自定义 collective ops）\n\n**风险：**\n\n- **高风险**：MoE 的 expert routing 在 Neuron 上如何高效实现不明确\n  - vLLM CPU/CUDA 后端用 `torch.topk` + `torch.scatter`，Neuron 可能不支持或性能差\n  - 可能需要自定义 XLA kernel 或依赖 Neuron Collective Communication\n- **需要深度理解**：\n  - Neuron 的 TP sharding 如何分配 experts（每个 rank 分几个 expert？）\n  - Load balancing loss 如何在训练和推理中处理\n  - Qwen3Moe 的具体 routing 策略（是否有 auxiliary loss？）\n\n**时间估算：**\n\n- 熟悉 vLLM-Neuron + XLA 算子：3-5 天\n- 实现基础 Qwen3Moe（无 MoE，只测 Attention）：1-2 天\n- 实现 MoE 层并调试：5-10 天\n- 编译优化 + 性能调优：3-5 天\n- **总计：2-3 周**（单人，假设有 Neuron 经验）\n\n### 方案 C：回退到 NxDI/transformers-neuronx（规避问题）\n\n**目标：** 放弃 vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0，使用旧版 Neuron SDK (NxDI/transformers-neuronx)\n\n**优点：**\n\n- transformers-neuronx 0.16.0 支持更广泛的 HF 模型（包括 Qwen3Moe）\n- 不需要修改任何源码\n- 已有工作经验（之前的脚本就是这个版本）\n\n**缺点：**\n\n- **vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 的性能优化全部丢失**：\n  - Segmented prefill (更快的长 context 处理)\n  - 改进的 KV cache 管理\n  - 更好的 TP 调度\n  - PagedAttention 支持\n- **API 格式不同**：\n  - transformers-neuronx 是 HF Transformers 接口，不是 OpenAI-compatible server\n  - 需要自己实现 HTTP server wrapper\n  - 无法直接替换现有的 OpenAI client 调用\n- **可能被弃用**：AWS 主推 vLLM-Neuron，transformers-neuronx 可能停止更新\n\n**何时选择此方案：**\n\n- 时间紧迫，无法等待 vLLM-Neuron 官方支持\n- 性能要求不高（batch=1, 吞吐不是瓶颈）\n- 愿意维护两套代码（vLLM 和 transformers-neuronx）\n\n### 推荐方案：**方案 A（Patch GptOss）+ 向 AWS 提 issue/PR**\n\n**理由：**\n\n1. **最小可行**：只需修改 3 个文件，~50 行代码改动\n2. **风险可控**：\n   - 条件逻辑清晰，不影响现有模型\n   - 如果 XLA kernel 不支持 `bias=None`，降级为传 `torch.zeros`（性能损失极小）\n3. **快速验证**：1-2 天可以完成 patch + 编译测试\n4. **向上游贡献**：\n   - 这是个通用问题（所有 bias-free 模型都遇到）\n   - AWS/vLLM-Neuron 团队很可能接受 PR\n   - 提 issue 后即使自己 patch，下个版本也会官方支持\n\n**执行计划：**\n\n1. **Phase 1**（1 天）：创建 patch 并挂载到容器\n2. **Phase 2**（1 天）：编译 Qwen3-32B (Judge) 验证 patch 正确性\n3. **Phase 3**（1 天）：编译 Tongyi-30B 验证 MoE 模型\n4. **Phase 4**（并行）：向 AWS Neuron GitHub 提 issue + PR\n\n**如果 Patch 失败的 Plan B：**\n\n- 临时使用 Llama-3.1-70B 替代 Tongyi（Llama 有 bias，GptOss 原生支持）\n- Judge 改用 Qwen3-14B（如果也失败，用 Llama-3.1-8B）\n- 等待 AWS 官方支持或升级到支持 Qwen3 的 vLLM 版本\n\n## Patch 实施细节（方案 A）\n\n### 文件修改 Diff\n\n#### 1. `config.py` 增加 attention_bias 字段\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass GptOssConfig:\n    # ... 现有字段 ...\n    \n    # NEW: Attention bias configuration\n    attention_bias: bool = True  # Whether attention layers have bias terms\n    mlp_bias: bool = True        # Whether MLP layers have bias terms (future-proofing)\n```\n\n在 `from_configs()` 中：\n```python\n# After filtered_dict line\nfiltered_dict["attention_bias"] = config_dict.get("attention_bias", True)\nfiltered_dict["mlp_bias"] = config_dict.get("mlp_bias", True)\n```\n\n#### 2. `model_bf16.py` 条件化 bias 创建\n\nAttention `__init__` (line ~398):\n```python\n# OLD:\nself.qkv_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(qkv_size, dtype=self.dtype))\nself.o_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(self.hidden_size, dtype=self.dtype))\n\n# NEW:\nif config.attention_bias:\n    self.qkv_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(qkv_size, dtype=self.dtype))\n    self.o_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(self.hidden_size, dtype=self.dtype))\nelse:\n    # Register as None so state_dict doesn\'t expect them\n    self.register_parameter(\'qkv_proj_bias\', None)\n    self.register_parameter(\'o_proj_bias\', None)\n```\n\nAttention `forward` 中所有 XLA kernel 调用（4 处）：\n```python\n# OLD:\nbias=self.qkv_proj_bias.unsqueeze(0),\n\n# NEW:\nbias=self.qkv_proj_bias.unsqueeze(0) if self.qkv_proj_bias is not None else None,\n```\n\n`load_weights()` mapping (line ~2267):\n```python\n# After qkv_proj_weight mapping\nif self.model.layers[0].self_attn.qkv_proj_bias is not None:\n    mappings[f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.qkv_proj_bias"] = [\n        f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.q_proj.bias",\n        f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.k_proj.bias",\n        f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.v_proj.bias",\n    ]\n    mappings[f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.o_proj_bias"] = (\n        f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.o_proj.bias"\n    )\n```\n\n#### 3. Weight loader 注册（line ~470-475）\n\n```python\n# OLD:\nset_weight_loader(self.qkv_proj_bias, qkv_bias_loader)\n\n# NEW:\nif self.qkv_proj_bias is not None:\n    set_weight_loader(self.qkv_proj_bias, qkv_bias_loader)\nif self.o_proj_bias is not None:\n    set_weight_loader(self.o_proj_bias, o_proj_bias_loader)\n```\n\n### 挂载方式（Docker Compose）\n\n在项目根目录创建 `docker/patches/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/` 并放置修改后的文件，然后在 `docker-compose.neuron.yml` 中：\n\n```yaml\nservices:\n  neuron:\n    image: public.ecr.aws/neuron/vllm-neuron:0.21.0\n    volumes:\n      - ./docker/patches/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss:/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss:ro\n```\n\n或通过 `docker run -v` 挂载。\n\n### 验证步骤\n\n1. **语法检查**：\n   ```bash\n   docker exec browsecomp-neuron python3 -m py_compile /opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/model_bf16.py\n   ```\n\n2. **加载测试**（不编译）：\n   ```bash\n   docker exec browsecomp-neuron python3 -c "\n   from vllm_neuron.model.gpt_oss import GptOssForCausalLM\n   print(\'Model class loaded successfully\')\n   "\n   ```\n\n3. **编译测试**（Qwen3-32B, 预计 30-60 分钟）：\n   ```bash\n   bash bash/neuron/compile_judge.bash\n   ```\n\n4. **服务测试**：\n   ```bash\n   bash bash/neuron/serve_judge.bash\n   curl http://localhost:8032/v1/completions -d \'{"model":"Qwen/Qwen3-32B","prompt":"Hello","max_tokens":10}\'\n   ```\n\n## 脚本重构方案（与 Patch 正交）\n\n无论 Patch 是否成功，脚本都需要重构以适配 vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 的配置格式。\n\n### 目标结构'}}]

vLLM（编译发生在首次加载时）\n"$PYTHON_BIN" -m vllm.entrypoints.openai.api_server \\\n    --model "$MODEL" \\\n    --tensor-parallel-size "$TP_SIZE" \\\n    --max-model-len "$MAX_MODEL_LEN" \\\n    --max-num-seqs "$MAX_NUM_SEQS" \\\n    --block-size "$BLOCK_SIZE" \\\n    --num-gpu-blocks-override "$NUM_GPU_BLOCKS_OVERRIDE" \\\n    --enable-prefix-caching \\\n    --additional-config "$ADDITIONAL_CONFIG" \\\n    --hf-overrides \'{"architectures": ["GptOssForCausalLM"]}\' \\\n    --port 9999\n\necho ""\necho "=== Compilation Complete ==="\necho "Artifacts: $NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS"\n```\n\n#### `serve_tongyi.bash` / `serve_judge.bash`\n\n类似 compile，但：\n- **不检查** artifacts 是否存在（vLLM 会自动检测并报错）\n- 使用 `exec` 启动（signal 正确传递，容器 stop 时优雅关闭）\n- PORT 从环境变量读取或默认值（Tongyi 默认 6008，Judge 默认 8032）\n- `--host 0.0.0.0` 允许外部访问\n\n```bash\n# ... 前面同 compile，直到 export 部分 ...\n\n# Port (overridable via environment)\nPORT="${PORT:-6008}"  # Tongyi: 6008, Judge: 8032\n\necho "=== <Model Name> Server (vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0) ==="\necho "Model:       $MODEL"\necho "Port:        $PORT"\necho "TP Size:     $TP_SIZE"\necho "Max Len:     $MAX_MODEL_LEN"\necho "Max Seqs:    $MAX_NUM_SEQS"\necho "Devices:     ${NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES:-auto}"\necho "Artifacts:   $NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS"\necho ""\n\nexec "$PYTHON_BIN" -m vllm.entrypoints.openai.api_server \\\n    --model "$MODEL" \\\n    --tensor-parallel-size "$TP_SIZE" \\\n    --max-model-len "$MAX_MODEL_LEN" \\\n    --max-num-seqs "$MAX_NUM_SEQS" \\\n    --block-size "$BLOCK_SIZE" \\\n    --num-gpu-blocks-override "$NUM_GPU_BLOCKS_OVERRIDE" \\\n    --enable-prefix-caching \\\n    --additional-config "$ADDITIONAL_CONFIG" \\\n    --hf-overrides \'{"architectures": ["GptOssForCausalLM"]}\' \\\n    --port "$PORT" \\\n    --host 0.0.0.0\n```\n\n#### `serve_tongyi_cluster.bash` / `serve_judge_cluster.bash`\n\n**仅用于大机器（trn2.6xlarge+，≥2 devices）**，在 trn2.3xlarge 上无需使用。\n\n保留 NUMA-aware 多副本结构，从 config 读取配置，为每个副本设置：\n- `NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES=<device_id>` — 每个副本绑定一个 Neuron device\n- `PORT=<base_port + replica_id>` — 不同端口\n- 调用 `serve_<model>.bash` 并后台运行\n\n**关键变化：**\n- `NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES` 使用 **device ID**（0, 1, ...），不是 core range\n- trn2.6xlarge (2 devices × 4 cores each) → 2 个副本，每个 TP=4\n- trn2.12xlarge (4 devices) → 4 个副本 (TP=4) 或 2 个副本 (TP=8) 或 1 个副本 (TP=16)\n\n```bash\n# Example for trn2.6xlarge (2 devices)\nNUM_REPLICAS=2\nBASE_PORT=6008\nDEVICES_PER_REPLICA=1  # Each replica uses 1 device (4 cores)\n\nfor i in $(seq 0 $((NUM_REPLICAS - 1))); do\n    export NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES=$i\n    export PORT=$((BASE_PORT + i))\n    bash bash/neuron/serve_tongyi.bash &\ndone\nwait\n```'}}]

[{'type': 'tool_use', 'id': 'toolu_bdrk_01CoPDe6i9zs1SJpG2mjJeEN', 'name': 'ExitPlanMode', 'input': {'plan': '# bash/neuron/ 脚本重构 - vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0\n\n## Context\n\n当前 bash/neuron/ 脚本基于旧版 vLLM-Neuron (NxDI/0.16.0) 编写，配置格式过时。需要迁移到 Docker 环境 (browsecomp-neuron:0.21.0) 和 vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0。\n\n**硬件：** trn2.3xlarge — 1 Neuron device × 4 cores，TP_SIZE 最大 = 4  \n**运行模式：** 三个模型分时运行（同时只跑一个）  \n**范围：** 只重构 compile 和 serve 脚本，n_tongyi.bash / n_tongyi_get.bash 暂不动\n\n**三个模型：**\n1. Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B (Qwen3MoeForCausalLM) — TP=4, 32K context\n2. Qwen3-32B (Judge, Qwen3ForCausalLM) — TP=4, 8K context\n3. Qwen3-Embedding-8B — Optimum Neuron（不走vLLM）\n\n### **关键阻塞问题：attention_bias 不兼容**\n\n**现状：**\n- vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 的模型注册表只有 4 个架构：`LlamaForCausalLM`, `GptOssForCausalLM`, `Eagle3LlamaForCausalLM`, `Qwen3VLForConditionalGeneration`\n- **不支持** `Qwen3MoeForCausalLM` (Tongyi) 和 `Qwen3ForCausalLM` (Judge)\n- 通过 `--hf-overrides \'{"architectures": ["GptOssForCausalLM"]}\'` 可以强制使用 GptOss 通用路径\n- **但是**：GptOss 的 Attention 层**无条件初始化** `qkv_proj_bias` 和 `o_proj_bias` 参数，并在权重加载时**硬编码映射**到 HF checkpoint 的 `q_proj.bias`, `k_proj.bias`, `v_proj.bias`, `o_proj.bias` 键\n- Qwen3 系列所有模型的 config 中 `attention_bias: False` — checkpoint 中**不存在这些 bias 张量**\n- 加载时报错：`RuntimeError: Checkpoint key(s) not found for parameter \'model.layers.0.self_attn.qkv_proj_bias\': [\'model.layers.0.self_attn.q_proj.bias\', ...]`\n\n**根本原因：**\n- `/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/model_bf16.py` line ~398: `self.qkv_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(qkv_size, dtype=self.dtype))` — 无条件创建\n- line ~2267: `mappings[f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.qkv_proj_bias"] = [q_proj.bias, k_proj.bias, v_proj.bias]` — 无条件映射\n- GptOss config (`/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/config.py`) **没有 `attention_bias` 字段**\n- **GptOss 模型设计时假设所有模型都有 attention bias**，不支持 bias-free 架构\n\n**vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 关键变化：**\n\n| 旧 (NxDI) | 新 (0.21.0) |\n|-----------|-------------|\n| `{"override_neuron_config": {...}}` | `{"neuron_config": {...}}` |\n| `context_encoding_buckets` | `num_batched_tokens_buckets` |\n| `prefix_buckets` | 移除（自动管理） |\n| `token_generation_buckets` | 隐式，由 max_model_len 决定 |\n| `NXD_COMPILE_MAX_WORKERS` | `VLLM_NEURON_PARALLEL_COMPILE_WORKERS` |\n| `NEURON_SCHEDULER=custom/native` | 移除，统一调度器 |\n| 无 | `on_device_sampling_config`（**必需**，async scheduling 默认开启）|\n| 无 | `kv_segment_size_buckets`（segmented prefill，**必须=num_batched_tokens_buckets**）|\n\n## 自开发支持 Qwen3 可行性分析\n\n### 方案 A：Patch GptOss 模型（最小改动）\n\n**目标：** 让 GptOss 支持 `attention_bias: False` 的模型\n\n**需要修改的文件：**\n\n1. **`/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/config.py`**\n   - 增加字段：`attention_bias: bool = True`\n   - 在 `from_configs()` 中从 HF config 读取：`filtered_dict["attention_bias"] = config_dict.get("attention_bias", True)`\n\n2. **`/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/model_bf16.py`**\n   - **Attention `__init__`** (line ~395-402): 条件化创建 bias\n     ```python\n     if config.attention_bias:\n         self.qkv_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(qkv_size, dtype=self.dtype))\n         self.o_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(self.hidden_size, dtype=self.dtype))\n     else:\n         self.qkv_proj_bias = None\n         self.o_proj_bias = None\n     ```\n   - **Attention `forward`** (line ~660-730): 条件化传递 bias（4处调用 `xla_attn`/`xla_attn_v3`）\n     ```python\n     bias=self.qkv_proj_bias.unsqueeze(0) if self.qkv_proj_bias is not None else None\n     ```\n   - **`load_weights`** (line ~2267-2280): 条件化映射\n     ```python\n     if config.attention_bias:\n         mappings[f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.qkv_proj_bias"] = [...]\n         mappings[f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.o_proj_bias"] = (...)\n     ```\n\n3. **`/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/weight_loaders_bf16.py`**\n   - `fused_qkv_bias_loader` 和权重加载器注册逻辑保持不变（当 bias=None 时不会调用）\n\n**实施方式：**\n\na. **Docker 镜像外部挂载 patch**（推荐，非侵入式）\n   - 在宿主机创建 `docker/patches/vllm_neuron/` 目录\n   - 复制原始文件并修改\n   - Docker compose 挂载：`-v ./docker/patches/vllm_neuron:/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron:ro`\n   - **优点**：不修改镜像，可版本控制，易于迭代\n   - **缺点**：每次拉新镜像需要重新验证 patch 兼容性\n\nb. **构建自定义 Docker 镜像**（生产级）\n   - `FROM public.ecr.aws/neuron/vllm-neuron:0.21.0`\n   - Dockerfile 中 `COPY patches/` + `RUN sed -i` 或直接 `COPY` 完整修改后的文件\n   - **优点**：自包含，可分发\n   - **缺点**：需要维护 Dockerfile，镜像体积增大\n\nc. **容器内运行时 patch**（调试用）\n   - `docker exec` 进容器，直接 `vim` 或 `sed -i` 修改文件\n   - **优点**：快速验证\n   - **缺点**：容器重启丢失，不可复现\n\n**风险评估：**\n\n- **低风险区域**：\n  - Config 增加字段（向后兼容，默认值 `True` 保持现有行为）\n  - Weight mapping 条件化（只影响 bias=False 的模型）\n  - Bias 初始化条件化（nn.Parameter 为 None 是合法的）\n\n- **中等风险**：\n  - Forward 中 XLA 算子调用改动 — 需要验证 `bias=None` 是否被 XLA kernel 支持\n  - 如果 `xla_attn` 不支持 `bias=None`，可能需要传 `torch.zeros_like(...)` 而非 None\n\n- **需要验证**：\n  - XLA attention kernel (`xla_attn`, `xla_attn_v3`) 是否支持 `bias=None` 或需要显式零张量\n  - Neuron 编译器是否会因 bias=None 优化掉相关计算\n  - TP 分片逻辑在 bias=None 时是否正常工作\n\n### 方案 B：实现独立 Qwen3Moe 模型类（完整支持）\n\n**目标：** 注册新的 `Qwen3MoeForCausalLM` 架构到 vLLM-Neuron\n\n**需要新增的文件：**\n\n1. **`/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/qwen3_moe/`**\n   - `config.py` — Qwen3Moe 配置（基于 GptOss 修改，增加 MoE 参数）\n   - `model_bf16.py` — Qwen3Moe 模型实现\n     - Attention 层：从 GptOss 复制并移除 bias\n     - **MoE 层**：需要实现 expert routing + top-k gating + load balancing\n   - `weight_loaders_bf16.py` — 权重加载器（复制 GptOss，移除 bias 映射）\n   - `factory.py` — 模型工厂\n   - `__init__.py` — 导出 `Qwen3MoeForCausalLM`\n\n2. **修改 `/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/registry.py`**\n   ```python\n   from .qwen3_moe import Qwen3MoeForCausalLM\n   models.append(("Qwen3MoeForCausalLM", Qwen3MoeForCausalLM))\n   ```\n\n**工作量：**\n\n- **Attention 层**：100 行（复制 GptOss，删 bias 逻辑）\n- **MoE 层**：300-500 行（expert routing, gating, load balancing, TP sharding）\n- **Config + 权重映射**：100 行\n- **XLA/Neuron kernel 适配**：未知（如果 MoE 需要自定义 collective ops）\n\n**风险：**\n\n- **高风险**：MoE 的 expert routing 在 Neuron 上如何高效实现不明确\n  - vLLM CPU/CUDA 后端用 `torch.topk` + `torch.scatter`，Neuron 可能不支持或性能差\n  - 可能需要自定义 XLA kernel 或依赖 Neuron Collective Communication\n- **需要深度理解**：\n  - Neuron 的 TP sharding 如何分配 experts（每个 rank 分几个 expert？）\n  - Load balancing loss 如何在训练和推理中处理\n  - Qwen3Moe 的具体 routing 策略（是否有 auxiliary loss？）\n\n**时间估算：**\n\n- 熟悉 vLLM-Neuron + XLA 算子：3-5 天\n- 实现基础 Qwen3Moe（无 MoE，只测 Attention）：1-2 天\n- 实现 MoE 层并调试：5-10 天\n- 编译优化 + 性能调优：3-5 天\n- **总计：2-3 周**（单人，假设有 Neuron 经验）\n\n### 方案 C：回退到 NxDI/transformers-neuronx（规避问题）\n\n**目标：** 放弃 vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0，使用旧版 Neuron SDK (NxDI/transformers-neuronx)\n\n**优点：**\n\n- transformers-neuronx 0.16.0 支持更广泛的 HF 模型（包括 Qwen3Moe）\n- 不需要修改任何源码\n- 已有工作经验（之前的脚本就是这个版本）\n\n**缺点：**\n\n- **vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 的性能优化全部丢失**：\n  - Segmented prefill (更快的长 context 处理)\n  - 改进的 KV cache 管理\n  - 更好的 TP 调度\n  - PagedAttention 支持\n- **API 格式不同**：\n  - transformers-neuronx 是 HF Transformers 接口，不是 OpenAI-compatible server\n  - 需要自己实现 HTTP server wrapper\n  - 无法直接替换现有的 OpenAI client 调用\n- **可能被弃用**：AWS 主推 vLLM-Neuron，transformers-neuronx 可能停止更新\n\n**何时选择此方案：**\n\n- 时间紧迫，无法等待 vLLM-Neuron 官方支持\n- 性能要求不高（batch=1, 吞吐不是瓶颈）\n- 愿意维护两套代码（vLLM 和 transformers-neuronx）\n\n### 推荐方案：**方案 A（Patch GptOss）+ 向 AWS 提 issue/PR**\n\n**理由：**\n\n1. **最小可行**：只需修改 3 个文件，~50 行代码改动\n2. **风险可控**：\n   - 条件逻辑清晰，不影响现有模型\n   - 如果 XLA kernel 不支持 `bias=None`，降级为传 `torch.zeros`（性能损失极小）\n3. **快速验证**：1-2 天可以完成 patch + 编译测试\n4. **向上游贡献**：\n   - 这是个通用问题（所有 bias-free 模型都遇到）\n   - AWS/vLLM-Neuron 团队很可能接受 PR\n   - 提 issue 后即使自己 patch，下个版本也会官方支持\n\n**执行计划：**\n\n1. **Phase 1**（1 天）：创建 patch 并挂载到容器\n2. **Phase 2**（1 天）：编译 Qwen3-32B (Judge) 验证 patch 正确性\n3. **Phase 3**（1 天）：编译 Tongyi-30B 验证 MoE 模型\n4. **Phase 4**（并行）：向 AWS Neuron GitHub 提 issue + PR\n\n**如果 Patch 失败的 Plan B：**\n\n- 临时使用 Llama-3.1-70B 替代 Tongyi（Llama 有 bias，GptOss 原生支持）\n- Judge 改用 Qwen3-14B（如果也失败，用 Llama-3.1-8B）\n- 等待 AWS 官方支持或升级到支持 Qwen3 的 vLLM 版本\n\n## Patch 实施细节（方案 A）\n\n### 文件修改 Diff\n\n#### 1. `config.py` 增加 attention_bias 字段\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass GptOssConfig:\n    # ... 现有字段 ...\n    \n    # NEW: Attention bias configuration\n    attention_bias: bool = True  # Whether attention layers have bias terms\n    mlp_bias: bool = True        # Whether MLP layers have bias terms (future-proofing)\n```\n\n在 `from_configs()` 中：\n```python\n# After filtered_dict line\nfiltered_dict["attention_bias"] = config_dict.get("attention_bias", True)\nfiltered_dict["mlp_bias"] = config_dict.get("mlp_bias", True)\n```\n\n#### 2. `model_bf16.py` 条件化 bias 创建\n\nAttention `__init__` (line ~398):\n```python\n# OLD:\nself.qkv_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(qkv_size, dtype=self.dtype))\nself.o_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(self.hidden_size, dtype=self.dtype))\n\n# NEW:\nif config.attention_bias:\n    self.qkv_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(qkv_size, dtype=self.dtype))\n    self.o_proj_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(self.hidden_size, dtype=self.dtype))\nelse:\n    # Register as None so state_dict doesn\'t expect them\n    self.register_parameter(\'qkv_proj_bias\', None)\n    self.register_parameter(\'o_proj_bias\', None)\n```\n\nAttention `forward` 中所有 XLA kernel 调用（4 处）：\n```python\n# OLD:\nbias=self.qkv_proj_bias.unsqueeze(0),\n\n# NEW:\nbias=self.qkv_proj_bias.unsqueeze(0) if self.qkv_proj_bias is not None else None,\n```\n\n`load_weights()` mapping (line ~2267):\n```python\n# After qkv_proj_weight mapping\nif self.model.layers[0].self_attn.qkv_proj_bias is not None:\n    mappings[f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.qkv_proj_bias"] = [\n        f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.q_proj.bias",\n        f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.k_proj.bias",\n        f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.v_proj.bias",\n    ]\n    mappings[f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.o_proj_bias"] = (\n        f"{layer_prefix}.self_attn.o_proj.bias"\n    )\n```\n\n#### 3. Weight loader 注册（line ~470-475）\n\n```python\n# OLD:\nset_weight_loader(self.qkv_proj_bias, qkv_bias_loader)\n\n# NEW:\nif self.qkv_proj_bias is not None:\n    set_weight_loader(self.qkv_proj_bias, qkv_bias_loader)\nif self.o_proj_bias is not None:\n    set_weight_loader(self.o_proj_bias, o_proj_bias_loader)\n```\n\n### 挂载方式（Docker Compose）\n\n在项目根目录创建 `docker/patches/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/` 并放置修改后的文件，然后在 `docker-compose.neuron.yml` 中：\n\n```yaml\nservices:\n  neuron:\n    image: public.ecr.aws/neuron/vllm-neuron:0.21.0\n    volumes:\n      - ./docker/patches/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss:/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss:ro\n```\n\n或通过 `docker run -v` 挂载。\n\n### 验证步骤\n\n1. **语法检查**：\n   ```bash\n   docker exec browsecomp-neuron python3 -m py_compile /opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/model_bf16.py\n   ```\n\n2. **加载测试**（不编译）：\n   ```bash\n   docker exec browsecomp-neuron python3 -c "\n   from vllm_neuron.model.gpt_oss import GptOssForCausalLM\n   print(\'Model class loaded successfully\')\n   "\n   ```\n\n3. **编译测试**（Qwen3-32B, 预计 30-60 分钟）：\n   ```bash\n   bash bash/neuron/compile_judge.bash\n   ```\n\n4. **服务测试**：\n   ```bash\n   bash bash/neuron/serve_judge.bash\n   curl http://localhost:8032/v1/completions -d \'{"model":"Qwen/Qwen3-32B","prompt":"Hello","max_tokens":10}\'\n   ```\n\n## 脚本重构方案（与 Patch 正交）\n\n无论 Patch 是否成功，脚本都需要重构以适配 vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 的配置格式。\n\n### 目标结构\n\n```\nbash/neuron/\n├── config/\n│   ├── tongyi.env                    # Tongyi 环境变量\n│   ├── tongyi_neuron_config.json     # Tongyi neuron_config\n│   ├── judge.env                     # Judge 环境变量\n│   ├── judge_neuron_config.json      # Judge neuron_config\n│   ├── embedding.env                 # Embedding 环境变量\n│   └── README.md                     # 配置指南（参数说明）\n├── compile_tongyi.bash               # 重写\n├── compile_judge.bash                # 重写（原 compile_qwen3_32b_judge.bash）\n├── compile_embedding.bash            # 轻微调整（从config读取）\n├── serve_tongyi.bash                 # 重写\n├── serve_judge.bash                  # 重写（原 serve_qwen3_32b_judge.bash）\n├── serve_embedding.bash              # 轻微调整（从config读取）\n├── serve_tongyi_cluster.bash         # 保留结构，更新调用（留给大机器）\n├── serve_judge_cluster.bash          # 同上（原 serve_qwen3_32b_judge_cluster.bash）\n├── n_tongyi.bash                     # 不动\n├── n_tongyi_get.bash                 # 不动\n├── run_tongyi_neuron.bash            # 不动\n├── evaluate_with_neuron_judge.bash   # 不动\n├── check_neuron_env.bash             # 不动\n├── download_*.bash                   # 不动\n└── archive-pre-dlc/                  # 已有归档\n```\n\n### 设计原则\n\n1. **配置分离**：所有参数在 `config/` 中，脚本从文件读取\n2. **用户自主配置**：用户编辑 .env 和 .json，无需改脚本\n3. **Docker 优先**：假设在容器中运行，保留 Docker 自动检测兼容宿主机\n4. **编译 worker ≤ 8**：默认 4（适配 4-core 机器内存）\n\n### 配置文件内容\n\n#### `config/tongyi.env`\n\n```bash\n# Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B (Qwen3MoeForCausalLM)\n# trn2.3xlarge: 1 device × 4 cores, TP=4 (core-level sharding)\nMODEL="Alibaba-NLP/Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B"\nTP_SIZE=4\nMAX_MODEL_LEN=32768\nMAX_NUM_SEQS=1\nBLOCK_SIZE=32\nNUM_GPU_BLOCKS_OVERRIDE=4000\n\n# Compilation\nVLLM_NEURON_PARALLEL_COMPILE_WORKERS=4\nNEURON_SKIP_EFA_AFFINITY=1  # Required: trn2.3xlarge has no EFA device\n\n# Paths\nNEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS="local-models/neuron-compiled-artifacts/tongyi-32k-tp4-v0.21.0"\nVLLM_CACHE_ROOT="local-models/vllm-cache"\nVLLM_NEURON_LOG_LEVEL=INFO\n\n# IMPORTANT: Do NOT set NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES for single-model runs\n# It will be set by cluster scripts for multi-replica deployments\n```\n\n#### `config/tongyi_neuron_config.json`\n\n```json\n{\n  "neuron_config": {\n    "num_batched_tokens_buckets": [2048],\n    "num_seqs_buckets": [1],\n    "kv_segment_size_buckets": [2048]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**说明：**\n- `num_batched_tokens_buckets: [2048]` — 必须等于 `max_num_batched_tokens` (MAX_NUM_SEQS × MAX_MODEL_LEN 的最小值，此处为 1 × 2048 = 2048)\n- `kv_segment_size_buckets` 必须等于 `num_batched_tokens_buckets`\n- 移除 `on_device_sampling_config` — vLLM 0.21.0 会自动配置\n\n#### `config/judge.env`\n\n```bash\n# Qwen3-32B Judge (Qwen3ForCausalLM)\n# trn2.3xlarge: 1 device × 4 cores, TP=4 (core-level sharding)\nMODEL="Qwen/Qwen3-32B"\nTP_SIZE=4\nMAX_MODEL_LEN=8192\nMAX_NUM_SEQS=1\nBLOCK_SIZE=128\nNUM_GPU_BLOCKS_OVERRIDE=2048\n\n# Compilation\nVLLM_NEURON_PARALLEL_COMPILE_WORKERS=4\nNEURON_SKIP_EFA_AFFINITY=1  # Required: trn2.3xlarge has no EFA device\n\n# Paths\nNEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS="local-models/neuron-compiled-artifacts/judge-8k-tp4-v0.21.0"\nVLLM_CACHE_ROOT="local-models/vllm-cache"\nVLLM_NEURON_LOG_LEVEL=INFO\n\n# IMPORTANT: Do NOT set NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES for single-model runs\n```\n\n#### `config/judge_neuron_config.json`\n\n```json\n{\n  "neuron_config": {\n    "num_batched_tokens_buckets": [512, 1024, 2048],\n    "num_seqs_buckets": [1],\n    "kv_segment_size_buckets": [512, 1024, 2048]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**说明：**\n- Judge 用于评估，通常输入较短，所以用多个 bucket 优化不同长度\n- 最大 bucket 2048 < MAX_MODEL_LEN 8192 是为了节省编译时间和内存（Judge 不需要满 8K 输入）\n- 如果需要完整 8K 支持，增加 `[4096, 8192]` bucket\n\n#### `config/embedding.env`\n\n```bash\n# Qwen3-Embedding-8B — Optimum Neuron\nMODEL="Qwen/Qwen3-Embedding-8B"\nTP_SIZE=4\nBATCH_SIZE=2\nSEQUENCE_LENGTH=1024\nINSTANCE_TYPE="trn2"\nEMBEDDING_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS="local-models/neuron-compiled-artifacts/qwen3-embedding-8b"\n```\n\n### 脚本模板\n\n#### `compile_tongyi.bash` / `compile_judge.bash`\n\n共同模式：\n\n```bash\n#!/usr/bin/env bash\nset -euo pipefail\n\nSCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"\nREPO_ROOT="$(cd "$SCRIPT_DIR/../.." && pwd)"\nCONFIG_DIR="$SCRIPT_DIR/config"\n\n# 1. 加载 config/<model>.env\nif [[ ! -f "$CONFIG_DIR/<model>.env" ]]; then\n    echo "Error: $CONFIG_DIR/<model>.env not found" >&2\n    exit 1\nfi\nsource "$CONFIG_DIR/<model>.env"\n\n# 2. Docker 检测\nif [[ -f /.dockerenv ]] || grep -q docker /proc/1/cgroup 2>/dev/null; then\n    PYTHON_BIN="${PYTHON_BIN:-python3}"\nelse\n    PYTHON_BIN="${PYTHON_BIN:-$REPO_ROOT/.venv/bin/python}"\nfi\n\n# 3. 读取 neuron_config JSON\nNEURON_CONFIG_FILE="$CONFIG_DIR/<model>_neuron_config.json"\nif [[ ! -f "$NEURON_CONFIG_FILE" ]]; then\n    echo "Error: $NEURON_CONFIG_FILE not found" >&2\n    exit 1\nfi\nADDITIONAL_CONFIG="$(cat "$NEURON_CONFIG_FILE")"\n\n# 4. 解析路径（相对→绝对）\n[[ "$NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS" == /* ]] || NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS="$REPO_ROOT/$NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS"\n[[ "$VLLM_CACHE_ROOT" == /* ]] || VLLM_CACHE_ROOT="$REPO_ROOT/$VLLM_CACHE_ROOT"\nmkdir -p "$NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS"\n\n# 5. 打印配置摘要\necho "=== <Model Name> Compilation (vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0) ==="\necho "Model:       $MODEL"\necho "TP Size:     $TP_SIZE"\necho "Max Len:     $MAX_MODEL_LEN"\necho "Max Seqs:    $MAX_NUM_SEQS"\necho "Workers:     $VLLM_NEURON_PARALLEL_COMPILE_WORKERS"\necho "Artifacts:   $NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS"\necho "Config:      $NEURON_CONFIG_FILE"\necho ""\necho "Neuron Config:"\ncat "$NEURON_CONFIG_FILE"\necho ""\necho ""\n\n# 6. export 环境变量\nexport VLLM_NEURON_PARALLEL_COMPILE_WORKERS\nexport NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS\nexport VLLM_CACHE_ROOT\nexport VLLM_NEURON_LOG_LEVEL\nexport NEURON_SKIP_EFA_AFFINITY\n# IMPORTANT: Do NOT export NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES here (single-model run)\n[[ -n "${NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES:-}" ]] && export NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES\n\n# 7. 启动 vLLM（编译发生在首次加载时）\n"$PYTHON_BIN" -m vllm.entrypoints.openai.api_server \\\n    --model "$MODEL" \\\n    --tensor-parallel-size "$TP_SIZE" \\\n    --max-model-len "$MAX_MODEL_LEN" \\\n    --max-num-seqs "$MAX_NUM_SEQS" \\\n    --block-size "$BLOCK_SIZE" \\\n    --num-gpu-blocks-override "$NUM_GPU_BLOCKS_OVERRIDE" \\\n    --enable-prefix-caching \\\n    --additional-config "$ADDITIONAL_CONFIG" \\\n    --hf-overrides \'{"architectures": ["GptOssForCausalLM"]}\' \\\n    --port 9999\n\necho ""\necho "=== Compilation Complete ==="\necho "Artifacts: $NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS"\n```\n\n#### `serve_tongyi.bash` / `serve_judge.bash`\n\n类似 compile，但：\n- **不检查** artifacts 是否存在（vLLM 会自动检测并报错）\n- 使用 `exec` 启动（signal 正确传递，容器 stop 时优雅关闭）\n- PORT 从环境变量读取或默认值（Tongyi 默认 6008，Judge 默认 8032）\n- `--host 0.0.0.0` 允许外部访问\n\n```bash\n# ... 前面同 compile，直到 export 部分 ...\n\n# Port (overridable via environment)\nPORT="${PORT:-6008}"  # Tongyi: 6008, Judge: 8032\n\necho "=== <Model Name> Server (vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0) ==="\necho "Model:       $MODEL"\necho "Port:        $PORT"\necho "TP Size:     $TP_SIZE"\necho "Max Len:     $MAX_MODEL_LEN"\necho "Max Seqs:    $MAX_NUM_SEQS"\necho "Devices:     ${NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES:-auto}"\necho "Artifacts:   $NEURON_COMPILED_ARTIFACTS"\necho ""\n\nexec "$PYTHON_BIN" -m vllm.entrypoints.openai.api_server \\\n    --model "$MODEL" \\\n    --tensor-parallel-size "$TP_SIZE" \\\n    --max-model-len "$MAX_MODEL_LEN" \\\n    --max-num-seqs "$MAX_NUM_SEQS" \\\n    --block-size "$BLOCK_SIZE" \\\n    --num-gpu-blocks-override "$NUM_GPU_BLOCKS_OVERRIDE" \\\n    --enable-prefix-caching \\\n    --additional-config "$ADDITIONAL_CONFIG" \\\n    --hf-overrides \'{"architectures": ["GptOssForCausalLM"]}\' \\\n    --port "$PORT" \\\n    --host 0.0.0.0\n```\n\n#### `serve_tongyi_cluster.bash` / `serve_judge_cluster.bash`\n\n**仅用于大机器（trn2.6xlarge+，≥2 devices）**，在 trn2.3xlarge 上无需使用。\n\n保留 NUMA-aware 多副本结构，从 config 读取配置，为每个副本设置：\n- `NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES=<device_id>` — 每个副本绑定一个 Neuron device\n- `PORT=<base_port + replica_id>` — 不同端口\n- 调用 `serve_<model>.bash` 并后台运行\n\n**关键变化：**\n- `NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES` 使用 **device ID**（0, 1, ...），不是 core range\n- trn2.6xlarge (2 devices × 4 cores each) → 2 个副本，每个 TP=4\n- trn2.12xlarge (4 devices) → 4 个副本 (TP=4) 或 2 个副本 (TP=8) 或 1 个副本 (TP=16)\n\n```bash\n# Example for trn2.6xlarge (2 devices)\nNUM_REPLICAS=2\nBASE_PORT=6008\nDEVICES_PER_REPLICA=1  # Each replica uses 1 device (4 cores)\n\nfor i in $(seq 0 $((NUM_REPLICAS - 1))); do\n    export NEURON_VISIBLE_DEVICES=$i\n    export PORT=$((BASE_PORT + i))\n    bash bash/neuron/serve_tongyi.bash &\ndone\nwait\n```\n\n#### `compile_embedding.bash` / `serve_embedding.bash`\n\n保持 Optimum Neuron 调用方式，仅改为从 `config/embedding.env` 读取参数。\n\n### 旧脚本处理\n\n将被重写的旧脚本先归档：\n```bash\nmv bash/neuron/compile_tongyi.bash bash/neuron/archive-pre-dlc/\nmv bash/neuron/compile_qwen3_32b_judge.bash bash/neuron/archive-pre-dlc/\nmv bash/neuron/compile_qwen3_embedding.bash bash/neuron/archive-pre-dlc/\nmv bash/neuron/serve_tongyi.bash bash/neuron/archive-pre-dlc/\nmv bash/neuron/serve_qwen3_32b_judge.bash bash/neuron/archive-pre-dlc/\nmv bash/neuron/serve_qwen3_embedding.bash bash/neuron/archive-pre-dlc/\nmv bash/neuron/serve_tongyi_cluster.bash bash/neuron/archive-pre-dlc/\nmv bash/neuron/serve_qwen3_32b_judge_cluster.bash bash/neuron/archive-pre-dlc/\nmv bash/neuron/serve_vllm_neuron.bash bash/neuron/archive-pre-dlc/\n```\n\n## 实施步骤\n\n1. **归档旧脚本** → archive-pre-dlc/\n2. **创建 config/ 目录和6个配置文件**\n3. **写 compile_tongyi.bash** — Tongyi 编译\n4. **写 compile_judge.bash** — Judge 编译\n5. **写 compile_embedding.bash** — Embedding 编译（从config读取）\n6. **写 serve_tongyi.bash** — Tongyi 单实例服务\n7. **写 serve_judge.bash** — Judge 单实例服务\n8. **写 serve_embedding.bash** — Embedding 服务（从config读取）\n9. **写 serve_tongyi_cluster.bash** — Tongyi 集群（大机器用）\n10. **写 serve_judge_cluster.bash** — Judge 集群（大机器用）\n\n## 最终建议和决策流程\n\n### 立即行动（并行执行）\n\n#### Track 1: Patch 开发（1-2 天）\n\n1. **创建 patch 文件**（1-2 小时）\n   - 复制 GptOss 源文件到 `docker/patches/vllm_neuron/model/gpt_oss/`\n   - 按上述 Diff 修改 `config.py`, `model_bf16.py`\n   - 验证语法：`python3 -m py_compile`\n\n2. **挂载 patch 并编译 Judge**（30-60 分钟编译 + 10 分钟测试）\n   - 挂载 patch 到容器\n   - `bash bash/neuron/compile_judge.bash`\n   - 如果编译成功 → Patch 有效，继续 Track 2\n   - 如果失败 → 分析错误，迭代 patch 或转 Plan B\n\n3. **编译 Tongyi**（30-60 分钟）\n   - `bash bash/neuron/compile_tongyi.bash`\n   - 验证 MoE 模型是否正常工作\n\n#### Track 2: 脚本重构（并行，不依赖 Patch）\n\n1. **创建配置文件**（30 分钟）\n   - `bash/neuron/config/` 目录\n   - 6 个配置文件 + README.md\n\n2. **重写 compile/serve 脚本**（2-3 小时）\n   - 8 个脚本（compile_×3, serve_×3, cluster_×2）\n   - 遵循上述模板\n\n3. **语法验证**（即时）\n   ```bash\n   jq . bash/neuron/config/*.json\n   bash -n bash/neuron/compile_*.bash\n   bash -n bash/neuron/serve_*.bash\n   ```\n\n#### Track 3: 向上游反馈（并行，低优先级）\n\n- 在 [aws-neuron/vllm-neuron GitHub](https://github.com/aws-neuron/neuronx-distributed) 提 issue\n- 标题：`[Feature Request] Support attention_bias=False models (Qwen3, Qwen3Moe)`\n- 附上：\n  - 错误日志\n  - 建议的 Patch diff\n  - 受影响的模型列表（Qwen3, Qwen3Moe, 可能还有其他 bias-free 模型）\n\n### Plan B（如果 Patch 失败）\n\n#### Option 1: 替换模型（保留 vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0）\n\n- **Tongyi-30B** → **Llama-3.1-70B** (有 attention_bias，GptOss 原生支持)\n  - 缺点：模型架构不同，可能影响实验结论\n  - 优点：vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 完整支持，性能最优\n\n- **Qwen3-32B Judge** → **Llama-3.1-8B Judge**\n  - 缺点：判别能力可能下降\n  - 优点：编译快，部署简单\n\n#### Option 2: 回退到 transformers-neuronx（放弃 vLLM）\n\n- 使用 NxDI 0.16.0 + transformers-neuronx\n- 缺点：\n  - 丢失 vLLM-Neuron 0.21.0 的性能优化\n  - API 不兼容（需要重写 HTTP wrapper）\n  - 可能被弃用\n- 优点：\n  - Qwen3Moe 原生支持\n  - 已有经验（之前的脚本）\n\n#### Option 3: 等待官方支持\n\n- AWS Neuron 团队通常 1-2 个月发布一次\n- 如果提 issue，可能在下个版本（0.22.0?）加入\n- 适合时间充裕的情况\n\n### 风险评估矩阵\n\n| 方案 | 成功概率 | 时间成本 | 性能损失 | 维护成本 |\n|------|---------|---------|---------|---------|\n| **Patch GptOss** | 70% | 1-2 天 | 0% | 低（等官方支持后移除） |\n| **替换模型 (Llama)** | 100% | 1 天 | 0% | 无 |\n| **回退 transformers-neuronx** | 100% | 3-5 天 | 20-30% | 高（维护两套代码） |\n| **等待官方支持** | 100% | 1-3 月 | 0% | 无 |\n\n### 推荐执行顺序\n\n1. **Day 1**：并行执行 Track 1 (Patch) + Track 2 (脚本重构)\n2. **Day 1 晚**：如果 Judge 编译成功 → 继续 Tongyi 编译\n3. **Day 2**：\n   - 如果 Patch 成功 → 完成脚本重构，开始实验\n   - 如果 Patch 失败 → 分析错误，决定是迭代 Patch 还是转 Plan B\n4. **Day 3+**：\n   - Plan B Option 1 (替换模型) — 最快\n   - Plan B Option 2 (回退 transformers-neuronx) — 需要更多开发\n\n**决策点：** Day 1 晚判断 Patch 成功率。如果 Judge 编译失败且错误不明确 → 立即转 Plan B Option 1（Llama）。\n\n## 验证计划\n\n### Phase 1: 语法和配置验证（Claude Code 立即完成）\n\n```bash\n# 配置文件语法\njq . bash/neuron/config/tongyi_neuron_config.json\njq . bash/neuron/config/judge_neuron_config.json\njq . bash/neuron/config/embedding.env >/dev/null && echo "embedding.env OK"\n\n# 脚本语法\nbash -n bash/neuron/compile_tongyi.bash\nbash -n bash/neuron/compile_judge.bash\nbash -n bash/neuron/compile_embedding.bash\nbash -n bash/neuron/serve_tongyi.bash\nbash -n bash/neuron/serve_judge.bash\nbash -n bash/neuron/serve_embedding.bash\nbash -n bash/neuron/serve_tongyi_cluster.bash\nbash -n bash/neuron/serve_judge_cluster.bash\n```\n\n### Phase 2: Patch 验证（用户手动，30-60 分钟）\n\n```bash\n# 1. 挂载 patch（如果使用 Docker）\ndocker run -v ./docker/patches/vllm_neuron:/opt/conda/lib/python3.13/site-packages/vllm_neuron ...\n\n# 2. 验证 patch 加载\ndocker exec browsecomp-neuron python3 -c "\nfrom vllm_neuron.model.gpt_oss import GptOssForCausalLM\nfrom vllm_neuron.model.gpt_oss.config import GptOssConfig\nprint(\'GptOss loaded, attention_bias field:\', hasattr(GptOssConfig, \'attention_bias\'))\n"\n\n# 3. 编译 Judge (最快验证)\nbash bash/neuron/compile_judge.bash\n# 预期：编译成功运行 >5 分钟无错误\n```\n\n### Phase 3: 完整编译（用户手动，2-3 小时）\n\n```bash\n# Judge (30-60 分钟)\nbash bash/neuron/compile_judge.bash\n\n# Tongyi (30-90 分钟，MoE 可能更慢)\nbash bash/neuron/compile_tongyi.bash\n\n# Embedding (10-20 分钟)\nbash bash/neuron/compile_embedding.bash\n```\n\n### Phase 4: 服务和推理测试（用户手动，10-20 分钟）\n\n```bash\n# 启动 Judge\nbash bash/neuron/serve_judge.bash &\nsleep 30  # 等待模型加载\n\n# 测试推理\ncurl http://localhost:8032/v1/completions \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "model": "Qwen/Qwen3-32B",\n Keep when porting.\n  # <-- MODEL-SPECIFIC: ...    Llama-specific. Change when porting.\n\nPARALLELISM SHARDING:\n  TP-only:  Attention heads sharded, MLP intermediate sharded\n  TP+DP:    Independent replicas per DP rank, same sharding as TP-only\n"""\n\nimport logging\nimport math\n\nimport torch\nfrom torch import nn\nfrom vllm.distributed.parallel_state import get_tp_group\nfrom vllm.model_executor.models.interfaces import SupportsEagle3\n\nimport vllm_neuron.functional as NF\nfrom vllm_neuron.model.kv_cache import KVSpec, LayerSpec\nfrom vllm_neuron.utils.checkpoints import SafetensorsCheckpoint\nfrom vllm_neuron.utils.dtype_utils import (\n    FP8_CLAMP_MAX,\n    validate_fp8_segmented_supported,\n)\nfrom vllm_neuron.utils.weight_loader import (\n    fused_qkv_weight_loader,\n    set_weight_loader,\n    sharding_weight_loader,\n    with_rank_override,\n)\n\nfrom transformers import PretrainedConfig\nfrom vllm_neuron.model.neuron_config import NeuronConfig\nfrom vllm_neuron.nn.sampler import Sampler\n\nimport vllm_neuron.nn as neuron_nn\nfrom vllm_neuron.nn.embedding import VocabDimShardedEmbedding\nfrom vllm_neuron.vllm.spec_decode.decorator import async_speculative_decoding\n\nfrom .config import LlamaConfig\nfrom .quantization import QuantScheme\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\n# =============================================================================\n# Section 1: RMS Normalization\n# <-- MODEL-SPECIFIC: Llama uses standard RMSNorm (no hidden dim padding)\n# =============================================================================\nclass LlamaRMSNorm(nn.Module):\n    """RMS Normalization.\n\n    <-- MODEL-SPECIFIC: Standard RMSNorm without padding. Other models may use\n    LayerNorm or RMSNorm with padded hidden dim.\n    """\n\n    def __init__(self, hidden_size: int, eps: float, dtype: torch.dtype):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.weight = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(hidden_size, dtype=dtype))\n        self.variance_epsilon = eps\n\n    def forward(self, hidden_states: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:\n        input_dtype = hidden_states.dtype\n        hidden_states = hidden_states.to(torch.float32)\n        variance = hidden_states.pow(2).mean(-1, keepdim=True)\n        hidden_states = hidden_states * torch.rsqrt(variance + self.variance_epsilon)\n        return (self.weight * hidden_states).to(input_dtype)\n\n\n# =============================================================================\n# Section 2: Rotary Position Embedding (Llama3 RoPE)\n# <-- MODEL-SPECIFIC: Llama uses Llama3-style RoPE scaling\n# =============================================================================\n\n\ndef _apply_rotary_emb(\n    x: torch.Tensor, cos: torch.Tensor, sin: torch.Tensor\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    """<-- MODEL-SPECIFIC: Interleaved RoPE (rotate_half style)."""\n    x1 = x[..., : x.shape[-1] // 2]\n    x2 = x[..., x.shape[-1] // 2 :]\n    rotated = torch.cat((-x2, x1), dim=-1)\n    return x * cos + rotated * sin\n\n\ndef apply_rotary_pos_emb(\n    q: torch.Tensor,\n    k: torch.Tensor,\n    cos: torch.Tensor,', 'is_error': False}]

## USER (2026-07-22 06:04:41)

[{'tool_use_id': 'toolu_bdrk_016FMjNSEEtWDdpB6kis1oNy', 'type': 'tool_result', 'content': 'class LlamaAttention(nn.Module):\n    """Multi-head attention with TP head sharding.\n\n    >>> PARALLELISM: TP <<<\n    - Q/K/V heads are sharded across TP ranks\n    - KV heads are replicated when fewer than TP size (GQA)\n    - Prefill: all-gather input → QKV proj → attention → O proj → reduce-scatter\n    - Decode: fused megakernel with TP all-reduce\n\n    <-- MODEL-SPECIFIC:\n    - GQA with separate Q and KV head counts\n    - No attention bias, no sinks, no sliding window\n    - Llama3 RoPE (rotate_half style)\n    """\n\n    def __init__(self, config: LlamaConfig, layer_idx: int):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.layer_idx = layer_idx\n        self.head_dim = config.head_dim\n        self.dtype = config.torch_dtype\n        self.hidden_size = config.hidden_size\n        self.num_attention_heads = config.num_attention_heads\n        self.num_key_value_heads = config.num_key_value_heads\n        self.scaling = config.head_dim**-0.5\n\n        # >>> PARALLELISM: TP group setup <<<\n        from vllm.distributed.parallel_state import get_dcp_group\n        from vllm_neuron.parallel.neuron_parallel_state import (\n            get_neuron_dcp_kv_group,\n            get_neuron_dcp_tp_group,\n        )\n\n        dcp_group = get_dcp_group()\n        self.dcp_size = dcp_group.world_size\n        self.dcp_group = dcp_group if self.dcp_size > 1 else None\n\n        dcp_kv_group = get_neuron_dcp_kv_group()\n        self.cp_kv_group = dcp_kv_group\n\n        self.apply_prefill_dcp = (\n            config.neuron_config.apply_prefill_dcp if config.neuron_config else False\n        )\n        if self.apply_prefill_dcp and self.dcp_size > 1:\n            # DCP prefill (Gather Q):\n            # - dcp_tp_group (size TP/DCP): different heads, same tokens → SP + weight sharding\n            # - cp_kv_group (size DCP): same heads, different tokens → AllGather Q + LSE\n            # - world_group (size TP): full SP gather to get all S tokens before slicing\n            dcp_tp_group = get_neuron_dcp_tp_group()\n            self.tp_group = dcp_tp_group\n            self.world_group = get_tp_group()\n            self.world_size = dcp_tp_group.world_size\n            self.rank = dcp_tp_group.rank_in_group\n        else:\n            # Standard TP: weights sharded across full TP.\n            self.tp_group = get_tp_group()\n            self.world_size = self.tp_group.world_size\n            self.rank = self.tp_group.rank_in_group\n\n        # DCP chunk index: which token group this rank belongs to.\n        # With TP=8, DCP=4, TP pairs [0,1],[2,3],[4,5],[6,7]:\n        # cp_chunk_idx = tp_rank // tp_pair_size = tp_rank // (TP/DCP)\n        full_tp_rank = get_tp_group().rank_in_group\n        full_tp_size = get_tp_group().world_size\n        tp_pair_size = full_tp_size // max(self.dcp_size, 1)\n        self.cp_chunk_idx = full_tp_rank // tp_pair_size if self.dcp_size > 1 else 0\n\n        # KV cache interleave size for DCP (read from vllm parallel config)\n        from vllm.config import get_current_vllm_config\n\n        vllm_config = get_current_vllm_config()\n        self.cp_kv_cache_interleave_size = getattr(\n            vllm_config.parallel_config, "cp_kv_cache_interleave_size", 1\n        )\n\n        # >>> PARALLELISM: Dependent DP setup (decode-only Q/O sharding across DP) <<<\n        self.attention_dp_size = (\n            config.neuron_config.attention_dp_size if config.neuron_config else 1\n        )\n        from vllm_neuron.parallel.neuron_parallel_state import (\n            get_neuron_attention_dp_group,\n            get_neuron_attention_dp_rank,\n        )\n\n        self.attention_dp_group = get_neuron_attention_dp_group()\n        self.attention_dp_rank = get_neuron_attention_dp_rank()\n\n        # >>> PARALLELISM: Attention TP supergroup (TP * attn_dp) <<<\n        from vllm_neuron.parallel.neuron_parallel_state import (\n            get_neuron_attention_tp_group,\n        )\n\n        self.attn_tp_group = get_neuron_attention_tp_group()\n\n        # Effective sharding degree for Q/O (TP for standard, TP*DDP for attention DP)\n        effective_q_shards = self.world_size * self.attention_dp_size\n\n        # >>> PARALLELISM: Head sharding calculation <<<\n        # Q heads per rank: sharded across TP*DDP for decode\n        self.num_attention_heads_per_rank = (\n            self.num_attention_heads // effective_q_shards\n        )\n\n        # KV heads per rank: determines cache size (always full TP amount).\n        # When num_kv_heads > TP and attention DP is enabled, KV weights are also sharded\n        # across attention DP (fewer projected heads). The cache stores the gathered result\n        # (full TP heads) so attention reads locally without a2a\'ing prior context.\n        self.kv_needs_a2a = (\n            self.attention_dp_size > 1\n            and self.num_key_value_heads > self.world_size\n            and self.num_key_value_heads % effective_q_shards == 0\n        )\n\n        # Cache sizing: full TP heads (unchanged by attention DP)\n        if self.world_size >= self.num_key_value_heads:\n            self.num_key_value_heads_per_rank = 1\n            self.num_kv_replicas = self.world_size // self.num_key_value_heads\n        else:\n            self.num_key_value_heads_per_rank = (\n                self.num_key_value_heads // self.world_size\n            )\n            self.num_kv_replicas = 1\n\n        # Weight sizing: may be smaller when KV is dependent-DP-sharded\n        self.num_kv_heads_for_weight = (\n            self.num_key_value_heads // effective_q_shards\n            if self.kv_needs_a2a\n            else self.num_key_value_heads_per_rank\n        )\n\n        self.num_key_value_groups = (\n            self.num_attention_heads_per_rank // self.num_kv_heads_for_weight\n        )\n\n        # Q/KV heads after all-to-all: each rank receives heads from all attention DP peers\n        self.num_q_heads_after_a2a = (\n            self.num_attention_heads_per_rank * self.attention_dp_size\n        )\n        self.num_kv_heads_after_a2a = (\n            self.num_kv_heads_for_weight * self.attention_dp_size\n            if self.kv_needs_a2a\n            else self.num_key_value_heads_per_rank\n        )\n\n        # >>> PARALLELISM: QKV weight shapes <<<\n        q_size = self.num_attention_heads_per_rank * self.head_dim\n        kv_size = self.num_kv_heads_for_weight * self.head_dim', 'is_error': False}]
